favorably on the appeal of the license the city council shall direct the city clerk to issue the license e notification of decision if the appeal of the license denial suspension or revocation is denied the applicant shall be immediately notified by registered or certified mail to the address provided on the application and the letter of notification shall state the basis for such denial f judicial review upon denial of the appeal of the license denial suspension or revocation by the city council an applicant may seek judicial review  582012 inspection of premises any sexually oriented business shall be deemed to have consented to periodic entry into and inspection of the business premises by appropriate city officials and inspection of only those business records necessary for the purpose of determining whether such business and persons are in compliance with this entry and inspection shall take place at any time the business is occupied or open for business  582012 standard of conduct and operation a it is unlawful for any sexually oriented business or any owner manager server entertainer or employee thereof or any customer or any sexually oriented business while on or about the premises of the business to fail to adhere to the standards of conduct and operation b standards applicable to all sexually oriented businesses the following standards apply to all sexually oriented business 1 establishment license all sexually oriented businesses shall post the license issued under this article in a conspicuous easily viewable location at eye level at the main cash register for the business and lighted in a manner for ease of inspection 2 manager on duty all sexually oriented businesses shall have a licensed manager on duty at all times the business is open to the public for any purpose and the managers name shall be posted in a conspicuous easily viewable location at eye level at the main cash register for the business and lighted in a manner for ease of inspection 3 employee records all sexually oriented businesses shall maintain a current list of all employees contract or otherwise along with their completed employment application and photo readily accessible for inspection within the premises 4 licenses available for managers and entertainers each manager issued a license under this article shall at all times when on the premises of the licensed business have said license in his possession the license for each entertainer shall be retained for ready inspection on the premises of the sexually oriented business 5 age restriction no person under the age of 18 years shall be permitted on the premises of any sexually oriented business 6 interior observation the interior of all sexually oriented businesses shall be configured in such a manner that offers and unobstructed view from the managers station of every area of the premises excluding restrooms 7 restrooms no restroom may contain any video equipment 8 security cameras parking areas surrounding the sexually oriented businesses shall be continually monitored and the recordings from security cameras shall be continually monitored and the recordings from security cameras shall be maintained for a period of at least 30 days 9 exterior observation the premises of all sexually oriented businesses shall be designed as to ensure that the interior of the premises is not observable from the exterior of the building 10 exterior display no sexually oriented business shall be conducted in any manner that permits the observation of sexually oriented entertainers engaged in sexually oriented entertainment or any depiction relating to specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas from any exterior source by display decoration sign show window or other openings 11 specified criminal acts and specified sexual activities prohibited no owner manager employee independent contractor server entertainer or customer shall engage in any specified criminal act or any specified sexual activity on the premises of the business 12 seminude or nude or simulated nudity no person including sexually oriented entertainers shall be seminude or in a state of seminudity or nude or in a state of nudity or in a state of simulated nudity while on the premises of a sexually oriented business licensed under this article 13 posting of age restriction a sign shall be posted at each entrance to a sexually oriented business stating it is unlawful for a person under 18 years old to enter this location c standards for sexually oriented media stores or retail stores sexually oriented media stores or retail stores shall be subject to the following additional standards 1 separate room if a business offers for sale or rent other media or merchandise sexually oriented media or merchandise shall be kept in a separate room physically and visually separate from the remainder of the store by an opaque wall reaching at least eight feet high or to the ceiling whichever is less 2 age limit no person under the age of 18 shall be permitted into a room containing sexually oriented media or sexually oriented merchandise 3 access if a business offers for sale or rent other media or merchandise access to the room containing sexually oriented media or sexually oriented merchandise shall be solid door accessed by an electronic control device controlled and monitored by a clerk visual control and posted with a sign clearly stating that no one under the age of 18 shall enter the room 4 location if a business offers for sale or rent other media or merchandise the entrance to the room containing the sexually oriented media or sexually oriented merchandise shall be located so that it is as far as reasonably practicable from media or merchandise likely to be of interest to children 5 room size any room wherein sexually oriented media or merchandise is offered for sale or rent shall be in an area containing at least 600 square feet and having no walls dividers curtains screens shades or other similar devices to obscure any part of the room from being monitored by the manager unless it is to separate the sexually oriented merchandise or media from nonsexuallyoriented merchandise or media 6 onsite entertainment prohibited at no time shall the store provide any type of sexually oriented onsite entertainment or show any type of sexually oriented electronic imagery on the premises 7 displays no displays of sexually oriented media merchandise or imager shall be visible from outside the room containing sexually oriented media or merchandise or from the exterior of the business 8 lighting any business that offers for sale or rent sexually oriented media or sexually oriented merchandise shall be well lit at a lighting level of at least 30 footcandles measured three feet from the floor 9 monitoring activities in any room having sexually oriented media or sexually oriented merchandise shall be monitored at all times by a store clerk video system located at the clerks counter d standards for sexually oriented motion picture theaters sexually oriented motion picture theaters shall be subject to the following additional standards 1 presentation area all screenings of motion pictures videos or other media shall occur in a room open to all customers of the establishment and containing at least 1000 square feet of floor area no walls dividers curtains screens shades or other similar devices shall be used to obscure any part of the screening room 2 lighting the lighting level in the area occupied by customers shall be at least five footcandles as measured at the floor 3 seating seating shall consist of individual theaterstyle chairs maximum seat width 20 inches with solid arms separating the chairs no couches benches portable chairs beds loose cushions or mattresses or other forms of seating shall be provided separate spaces for wheelchairs shall be provided in accordance with the applicable provisions of the building code and the americans with disabilities act 4 sexually oriented merchandise or media no sexually oriented motion picture theatre shall sell or rent sexually oriented merchandise or media e standards for a sexually oriented cabaret or nightclub sexually oriented cabaret and nightclubs shall be subject to the following additional standards 1 room all customerrelated activities and entertainment shall take place in a room of at least 600 square feet and in a room that has an unobstructed view by all persons from any part of such room 2 stage all sexually oriented entertainment shall take place on stage elevated at least 18 inches above the surrounding floor area with a minimum area of 90 square feet and with a horizontal separation of at least 60 inches between the edge of the stage and the nearest space to which customers have access the horizontal separation shall be physically enforced by a partial wall rail or other physical barrier measuring a minimum of four feet in height 3 access the manager or sexually oriented entertainer shall prohibit any person other than a licensed entertainer to occupy the stage area 4 tip all tips for sexually oriented entertainment shall be collected in containers that are accessible to customers 5 lighting the lighting level in the area occupied by customers shall be at least 15 footcandles as measured three feet from the floor 6 seating seating shall consist of chairs or open booths no couches beds loose cushions or mattresses or other forms of seating shall be provided 7 sexually oriented merchandise or media no sexually oriented cabaret or nightclub or motion picture theatre shall sell or rent sexually oriented merchandise or media 8 security at all times the business is open and for an hour after closing there shall be on site a licensed peace officer employed by the business owner who holds a valid and current license in good standing issued by the state commission on law enforcement officer standards and education the peace officers duty shall be to assist in maintaining order and to report criminal activity or behavior  582012 enforcement and penalties a the city may enforce this article by any restraint of dogs and cats  impoundment vtca health and safety   quarantine of animals vtca health and safety et seq article i  in general definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this chapter shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning animal means live vertebrate creatures domestic or wild animal control officer means any person designated by the city who is qualified to perform the duties required by this chapter or state law cat means a domestic feline of either sex including one neutered or sterilized dog means a domestic canine of either sex including one neutered or sterilized domestic animal includes all species of animals commonly and universally accepted as being domesticated fowl includes chickens turkeys ducks geese peacocks pheasants and any other member of the gallinaceous bird species or family including but being not limited to other domesticated or wild animals harboring means the act of keeping and caring for an animal or of providing a premises to which the animal returns for food shelter or care for a period of three days owner means any person who has the right of property in an animal or who harbors an animal or allows an animal to remain about his premises for a period of three days pet animal includes dogs and cats rabies vaccination means the vaccination of a dog cat or other domestic animal with an antirabies vaccine approved by the state department of health and the united states department of agriculture and administered by a veterinarian licensed by this state residence as related to the keeping of dogs and cats includes any building designed for or used as a dwelling whether temporary or permanent restraint means the securing of an animal by a leash or lead or by physical confinement within the real property limits of its owners running at large means an animal not under the physical control of the owner or his authorized representative an animal within an automobile or other vehicle of its owner shall not be deemed running at large the term running at large includes any animal staked tied or hobbled in such a manner as to allow such animal to go or get upon private property without authorization adjacent public sidewalk street alley or other public way stock pen includes any lot or pen in which more than two head of livestock are kept stray animal means any animal for which there is no identifiable owner or harborer vicious animal means any animal that commits an unprovoked attack upon a person on public or private property or in a public place wild animal includes all species of animals which exist in a natural unconfined state and are usually not domesticated  420     chief of police to enforce the chief of police or his designee is designated as the local health authority for purposes of enforcing rabies regulations and as the animal control officer within the city limits for the purpose of enforcing this chapter    state law reference animal control officer defined vtca health and safety interference with the animal control officer it is unlawful for any person to interfere with hinder or prevent the animal control officer or his designee in the enforcement of this chapter    animals running at large a nuisance it is unlawful for any owner to harbor any dog cat or other pet animal that by any sound or cry or other activity shall disturb the peace comfort or property of the inhabitants of the neighborhood and such disturbance is declared to be a public nuisance b confinement during estrus any unspayed female dog or cat in the stage of estrus heat shall be confined during such period of time in a house building or secure enclosure and the area of enclosure shall be so constructed that no other dog or cat may gain access to the confined animal owners who do not comply shall be ordered to remove the animal in heat to a boarding kennel or veterinary hospital all expenses incurred as a result of the confinement shall be paid by the owner failure to comply with the removal order of the animal control officer shall be a violation of this chapter and the dog or cat will then be impounded as prescribed in this chapter c injured animals animals injured on public property may be impounded and given adequate veterinary medical treatment pending notification of the owner if the injured animal is treated or impounded the owner of such animal shall be liable for all expenses of the treatment or the impoundment d restraint of pets and domestic animals pets and domestic animals shall be prohibited from running at large no owner of a pet or domestic animal shall fail to keep such animal under restraint at all times      state law reference authority of municipality to impound stray dogs and cats vtca health and safety   authority of municipalities to require restraint of dogs and cats vtca health and safety vicious animals a harboring prohibited  authority to impound no person shall own or harbor a vicious animal within the city such an animal shall be impounded as a public nuisance if impoundment of the animal running at large cannot be made with safety to the animal control officer or other persons the animal may be destroyed without notice to the owner or harborer b affidavit before municipal judge  procedure whenever affidavit shall be made before the judge of the municipal court that any dog has bitten attempted to bite or attacked any person in a vicious manner in the city and it shall appear that the person so bitten attempted to be bitten attacked or attempted to be attacked in a vicious manner as provided in this chapter was not at the time trespassing upon the property of the owner and not otherwise at fault then the judge of the municipal court shall upon proof thereof find the owner guilty of violating this section in addition if it is proven that the dog has bitten any person the judge may direct the owner of the dog to present the dog to a veterinarian or other public health authorities for rabies observation if such dog owner fails or refuses to do so within 24 hours after receiving the order the failure or refusal shall constitute a separate violation of this section c guard dogs it is unlawful to place or maintain any dog that has been specifically trained to attack in any area for the protection of persons or property unless the dog is physically confined to a specific area or is under complete and absolute control    impounded animals a impoundment animals owned or harbored in violation of this chapter or any other ordinance or law of this state shall be taken into custody by an animal control officer or other designated official and impounded stray animals shall be similarly impounded b animal shelter a suitable animal shelter shall be provided for the purpose of boarding and caring for any animal impounded under the provisions of this chapter the facility will conform to requirements of the state department of health c removal of animals from animal shelter it is unlawful for any person to remove any impounded animal from the animal shelter without the consent of the animal control officer or designated official or agency d removal of biting dogs and cats from confinement the impoundment of dogs and cats that have inflicted human bites shall be for a period of ten days for observation and shall not be terminated until consent from the proper officer or agency is secured confinement shall be at the owners expense e disposition of impounded unvaccinated dogs and cats the owner of a dog or cat that has not been properly vaccinated for rabies may reclaim the dog or cat within three days of pickup by paying to the city a pickup fee and a fee for food and housing per day or part of day thereafter as set from time to time by the council in the manual of fees and service charges of the city plus having the dog or cat vaccinated against rabies at the owners expense this does not prohibit charges being billed for harboring a nonvaccinated animal any animal impounded under this provision for over three days may be euthanized by the city f disposition of impounded vaccinated dogs and cats rabies vaccinated dogs and cats impounded under this section shall be held at the animal shelter for a period of not less than three days after notice to owner if the owner is known unless reclaimed by the owner dogs and cats whose owner is unknown and cannot be reasonably determined shall be held for a period of not less than three days the animal control officer will attempt to notify the animal owner of such impoundment as per information on the metal tag attached to its collar or harness the owner may reclaim the animal upon payment to the city of a pickup fee and a fee for food and housing per day or part of day thereafter as provided in the city fee schedule any animal impounded four days or more may be euthanized by the city euthanization does not relieve the animal owner of liability for costs associated with impoundment or in any way affect proceedings and penalties for violation of this chapter    state law reference treatment of impounded animals vtca livestock owned or controlled by such person to run at large within the city    livestock lots or pens permitted it is unlawful for any person to establish or maintain any horse lot mule lot or stock pen within a distance of 300 feet of any private residence unit in the city    swine prohibited it is unlawful for anyone to keep live swine within the city    keeping of fowl restricted a it is unlawful for any person to keep possess or maintain in the city any fowl or any pens enclosures or other structure in which any such fowl are kept or possessed within 50 feet of any church school day care center hospital nursing home or place of business and 25 feet from a residence other than the residence of the keeper possessor or owner of such fowl b the distance in feet is to be measured in a straight line from the nearest point of any pen enclosure or other such structure in which fowl are kept to the nearest point of such actual residence or place of human habitation church school day care center hospital nursing home or business c such enclosure or pen shall be located a minimum of five feet from the property line of the keeper possessor or owner of such fowl d it is unlawful to keep locate possess or maintain upon any property or enclosure more than 20 fowl per parcel of land one acre or less in size or 20 fowl per each additional acre of any combination of chickens turkeys geese ducks or other fowl e all fowl within the city limits shall be kept in an enclosure or pen constructed of material designed to keep fowl from escaping from the enclosure or pen it is unlawful for any person to keep harbor maintain or permit any person to keep harbor possess maintain or permit the presence on any lot or parcel of land within the city more than one of any fowl of any kind sex or description for each ten square feet of ground area available for such purpose f whenever and wherever fowl are kept located and maintained within the city limits the premises upon which the fowl are located shall be kept in such a manner as to prevent or eliminate the existence of any infectious type disease or conditions conducive to causing same or any odor offensive to persons g fowl or livestock that are part of a supervised youth project such as ffa 4h or others may be considered for an exception to the provisions listed in this article on the authority of the animal control officer and under conditions approved by the animal control officer and police chief  46   nuisances any fowl or livestock shall be declared a public nuisance and the keeping of such animals deemed unlawful if 1 the animals are allowed or permitted to run at large  2 by loud unusual or untimely crowing cackling honking gobbling or other sound the animals cause the peace and quiet of the neighborhood or the occupants of the adjacent premises to be disturbed or render the enjoyment of life and property uncomfortable or interfere with public peace and comfort  3 the owner or person in control of the animals endangers the public health or annoys neighbors by allowing the accumulation of droppings and putrescible materials that cause foul or offensive odors  or 4 the owner or person in control of the animals allows any condition to exist that causes a substantial or unreasonable interference with the use and enjoyment of anothers property    secs 836858  reserved article iii months of age or older shall have such animal vaccinated against rabies and annually thereafter any person moving into the city from a location outside of the city shall comply with this article within 30 days after having moved into the city b rabies vaccination withheld in dog bite cases if the dog or cat has inflicted a bite on any person or another animal within the last ten days the owner of the dog or cat shall report such fact to the veterinarian and no rabies vaccine shall be administered until after the tenday observation period c certificate of vaccination upon vaccination the veterinarian shall execute and furnish to the owner of the dog or cat as evidence thereof a certificate of vaccination the veterinarian shall retain a duplicate copy such certificate shall contain the following information 1 the name address and telephone number of the owner of the vaccinated dog or cat 2 the date of vaccination 3 the type of rabies vaccine used 4 the year and number of the rabies tag 5 the breed age color and sex of the vaccinated dog or cat d rabies tags concurrent with the issuance and delivery of the certificate of vaccination referred to in subsection c of this section the owner of the dog shall cause to be attached to the collar or harness of the vaccinated dog a metal tag serially numbered to correspond with the vaccination certificate number and bearing the year of issuance and the name of the veterinarian or his business name such tag shall be worn by the dog at all times e duplicate tags in the event of loss or destruction of the original tag provided in subsection d of this section the owner of the dog shall obtain a duplicate tag f proof it is unlawful for any person who owns or harbors a vaccinated dog or cat to fail or refuse to duty to report any person having knowledge that a dog or cat has bitten a human shall immediately report the incident to the animal control officer or city police department b confinement of dogs and cats any dog or cat that has bitten a person shall be put under quarantine for observation for a period of ten days from the date of the bite such quarantine shall consist of strict confinement in a cage or other secure enclosure that prevents any contact between the quarantined animal and any other animal the quarantine shall be at a veterinary hospital provided such facility is approved by the state department of health or at the city animal shelter if designated as an approved facility such confinement shall be at the expense of the owner of the animal stray dogs or cats whose owner cannot be ascertained shall be confined in the city animal shelter and will be disposed of by the city following the quarantine period the owner of any dog or cat that has been reported to have inflicted a bite on any person shall on demand produce the dog or cat for impoundment as prescribed in this section refusal to produce the dog or cat constitutes a violation of this section and each day of such refusal shall constitute a separate and individual violation c removal of dogs and cats from confinement it is unlawful for any person to remove from any place of confinement any dog or cat which has been confined as authorized without the consent of the impounding agency      buildings and construction footnotes  1  editors note see chapter 52 zoning for provisions regarding building permits there is a conflict between a general requirement and a specific requirement the specific requirement shall be applicable referenced standards standards referenced in the text of the technical codes shall be considered an integral part of the codes if specific portions of a standard are denoted by code text only those portions of the standard shall be enforced where code provisions conflict with a standard the code provisions shall be enforced permissive and advisory provisions in a standard shall not be construed as mandatory requirements not covered by code any requirements necessary for the strength stability or proper operation of an existing or proposed building structure electrical gas mechanical or plumbing system or for the public safety health and general welfare not specifically covered by this of the other technical codes shall be determined by the building official alternate materials and methods the provisions of the technical codes are not intended to prevent the use of any material or method of construction not specifically prescribed by them provided any such alternate has been reviewed by the building official the building official shall approve any such alternate provided the building official finds that the alternate for the purpose intended is at least the equivalent of that prescribed in the technical codes in quality strength effectiveness fire resistance durability and safety the building official shall require that sufficient evidence or proof be submitted to substantiate any claim made regarding the alternate secs 10101036  reserved article ii  additional local requirements division 1  generally barbed wire fences it is unlawful for any person to make or erect or cause to be made or erected within the city any barbed wire fence or any fence of similar material around or upon any lot owned by him or in his charge    secs 10381062  reserved division 2  electrical when electrical permit is not required notwithstanding any requirement for electrical permits provided in any of the building and technical codes adopted by the city in this chapter no permit is required for 1 the installation of electric wiring devices or equipment installed for or by the electric department of the city or for or by a public utility corporation operating under a franchise from the city to transmit and sell electric energy provided that such wiring devices or equipment are for the use of the electric department or the corporation in its operation as a public utility as provided for in its franchise 2 the replacement of any electrical fixtures or appliances that requires no change in the electric wiring for such fixture or appliance 3 the installation of wiring devices or equipment for communications or any signaling systems operating at 50 volts or less    electrical work that may be performed by persons not registered as contractors the following acts work and conduct shall be expressly permitted in the city without necessity of registration as a contractor under this chapter 1 electrical work done by a property owner on property owned and occupied or to be occupied as the property owners homestead  provided however that all such work or service shall be subject to permit inspection and approval in accordance with the terms of this chapter and the codes adopted hereunder 2 installation of service entrance only to a manufactured home performed by occupanthomeowner subject to permit inspection and approval 3 electrical work done by persons engaged by any public service company in the construction and maintenance of their public utility systems    tampering with public electrical service equipment it is unlawful for any person to cut move or attach to any wire switch or other property belonging to or controlled by any public service corporation or municipal electric department or cause the same to be done unless by permission from such corporation or municipal electric department so owning such wire switch or other property    liability for damage this division shall not be construed to relieve from or lessen the responsibility of any person installing operating or controlling any electric wiring or electrical apparatus for damages to anyone thereby or for full and faithful performance of the contract nor shall the city be held as assuming any liability by reason of the inspection authorized herein or certificate or permit issued pursuant to the provisions of this division this division shall also not be construed to relieve the electrician of his responsibility for any defective work that may have been concealed or escaped the notice of the electrical inspector    meters and circuits a the city electric department shall designate the location of the meter dwelling meter loops shall be at an outside point which will be readily accessible to meter readers and testers at all times meter loops for other than residence occupancy shall be at a point readily accessible to meter readers and testers during all business hours and shall be outside the building except by special permission from the city electric superintendent b where possible all meter loops shall be so placed and maintained that no meter dial will be more than 612 nor less than 512 feet above the permanent standing surface below the meter dial the meter loop location shall provide free space for testing and servicing of not less than 24 inches in front of each meter and not less than 24 inches in width and in no case of less width than the total width of all meters and metering equipment at each location no meter loop shall be placed in a washroom toilet room storage closet or any similar location or over plumbing fixtures machinery or other interfering obstructions c where two or more meter outlets are grouped or are on the same building each meter outlet shall be neatly and permanently marked to show the location it serves where one or more meter outlets are added to a group or on a building the person making the addition shall identify the old and the added outlets d electricians shall install the complete meter loop ready to attach the service with the exception of larger customers where the city electric department may install the necessary current or potential transformers e required service disconnection means shall be readily accessible and located outdoors immediately after the meter on all services rated at 200 amps or less      secs 10681090  reserved division 3  fuel gas shut off and disconnection for violations and unsafe conditions a at the direction of the gas inspector the company distributing gas in the city shall refuse to furnish gas or gas service to any house building or structure in the city and shall shut off and disconnect its gas supply or gas connection at any time and in any manner when it may appear to the gas inspector that the installation of any house piping appliances fixtures or apparatus or the construction or maintenance of same is unsafe or in violation of this chapter b the gas inspector is authorized and empowered to shut off the gas supply when such conditions appear to exist and shall notify the gas company and consumer of his action and no person shall again turn on the gas supply except with the permission of the gas inspector  however nothing herein shall be construed so as to relieve the gas consumer from the obligation of making all gas installations and connections in compliance with the provisions hereof    751927 approval of gas inspector required for gas turnon  issuance of certificate of approval a it is unlawful for any gas company its agents or employees to turn natural gas into the pipes in any building or on any premises situated in the city until it has been furnished a certificate from the gas inspector as herein provided for b should the gas inspector find that the gas fixtures and fittings on the premises and in the building have been installed in the manner provided for herein he shall issue a certificate of approval the same to be in triplicate and officially signed by him giving authority for the turning on of natural gas into the pipes in such building and on such premises one certificate shall be furnished to the gas company supplying natural gas one to the owner of the premises and building and one to be kept on file in the office of the city secretary  585   7527 secs 109310112  reserved division 4  unsafe building abatement code definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this division shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning building means any structure or part thereof erected for the support shelter enclosure of persons animals chattels or property of any kind building official means the designated authority charged with the administration of the building inspection department or his duly authorized representative official means the designated authority charged with enforcement of this division or his duly authorized representative dwelling means any building which contains one or more dwelling units used intended or designed to be built used rented leased let or hired out to be occupied or which is occupied for living purposes dwelling unit means a single unit providing complete independent living facilities for one or more persons including permanent provisions for living sleeping eating cooking and sanitation habitable room means a space in a structure for living sleeping eating or cooking bathrooms closets storage or utility rooms and similar rooms are not considered habitable rooms nuisance includes but is not limited to the following 1 any public nuisance known at common law or in equity jurisprudence  2 any attractive nuisance which may prove detrimental to others whether a structure in a building on the premises of a building or lot this includes any abandoned excavations wells shafts basements or cellars abandoned refrigerators appliances building materials trash or debris or structurally unsound structures  3 that which is dangerous to life or detrimental to health  or 4 any condition which causes a substantial or unreasonable interference with the use and enjoyment of ones property structure means that which is built or constructed an edifice or building of any kind any piece of work artificially built up or composed of parts joined together in some definite manner or any part thereof unsafe building means any building or structure that has any of the following conditions 1 the building structure or portion thereof is liable to fully or partially collapse 2 the structure or any part thereof was constructed or maintained in violation of any provision of an applicable city building code or any other applicable ordinance law or code of the city county or state 3 any means of egress or portion thereof that is of inadequate size or arrangement dilapidated in a state of disrepair or inoperable such that means of egress could be rendered unsafe in case of fire or panic 4 the foundation or any structural members are 25 percent or more damaged deteriorated improperly anchored or stressed or ineffective in supporting the imposed loads or maintaining proper clearances from finish grade as required by the minimum standards for housing 5 any walls or other vertical structural members which list lean or buckle to such an extent that a plumb line passing center of gravity falls outside the middle third of its base 6 the nonsupportive protective coverings of walls roofs ceilings or floors are 50 percent or more damaged or deteriorated or ineffective in protecting the structure or inhabitants from weather vermin insects decay or other causes of structural damage or disease 7 the structure or any part thereof has been damaged by fire water earthquake wind vandalism or other cause to such an extent that it has become either a nuisance or dangerous to the public health safety or welfare 8 any structure or part thereof that is in such a condition as to constitute a nuisance 9 the structure has inadequate lighting ventilation or sanitation facilities as required by state or local authorities for certain occupancies 10 the structure or any part thereof is designed for or being used or occupied in the commission of a crime 11 the structure or any part thereof is a fire hazard or is substandard dilapidated or otherwise unfit for human habitation and is a hazard to public health safety or welfare 12 any unsecured unoccupied building 13 any residential lot dwelling or dwelling unit not in full compliance with the citys minimum standards for housing unsecured unoccupied building means any structure which currently has no legitimate occupant or tenant and which has missing unlocked or inoperable doors windows or other unsecured openings into the building unauthorized entry can be made 04   minimum standards for housing  responsibility of owner no person shall occupy or permit to occupy any dwelling or dwelling unit for the purpose of living sleeping cooking or eating which is not in compliance with any of the following minimum requirements 1 property standards a all residential lots shall be free of holes excavations sharp protrusions or other objects or conditions reasonably capable of causing injury to a person b all wells cesspools or cisterns shall be securely covered or closed c proper drainage shall be provided to prevent standing water or flooding on the land d all dead trees or tree limbs that are reasonably capable of causing injury shall be removed e all water and sewer lines or conduits shall be properly maintained in a clean and sanitary working condition and free of leaks as required by state and local plumbing standards f property shall be kept clear of any open storage of vehicle parts used tires ice boxes refrigerators water heaters stoves ovens glass building material rubbish rubble garbage and similar material g in addition property shall be kept clear of any junked vehicles as defined by vtca transportation  2 structural standards a in all apartments apartment houses dwellings and dwelling units there shall be provided safe unobstructed and adequate means of egress leading to a safe and open area at ground level every bedroom shall have at least one window or opening which can easily be opened and facing directly to the outside the total of openable window or opening area in every bedroom leading outside shall be not less than 57 square feet b all dwellings and dwelling units shall have appropriate and adequate protection from deterioration and exposure to the elements which shall include but not be limited to paint waterproofing and properly installed siding wall coverings roofing ceilings flooring and flashing without holes cracks rot insect damage leaks or any other condition which could cause damage to the structure or parts c railings and flooring for stairs steps balconies porches and elsewhere shall be maintained and free of holes rot cracks and decay so as to be a safe means of egress in panic or emergency d attics basements cellars and crawl spaces shall be adequately ventilated and properly drained as specified in the city building code floor and wall framing members subject to rot or insect damage of any dwelling shall maintain a clearance to ground of not less than 16 inches except for girders which shall maintain a clearance to ground of not less than ten inches e fireplaces flues heat exchangers chimneys and other exhaust venting shall be in proper working order and maintain proper clearances from combustible material f broken or missing windows holes breaks and loose surface materials on floors walls and ceilings shall be properly repaired or replaced with like materials g all exterior doors windows skylights and associated locks and hardware shall be weathertight and kept in good working order h ceiling height in any room of any dwelling shall be not less than seven feet from finish floor level 3 utility standards a each occupied dwelling unit shall have all required plumbing fixtures properly maintained and connected to the public water and sewer as provided in the citys building and technical codes b each occupied dwelling unit within 300 feet of available electric utility supply shall have all required electrical outlets and equipment connected to such electric supply c heating equipment which is capable of maintaining a constant temperature of at least 68 degrees fahrenheit throughout any dwelling or a utility connection for such equipment in each habitable room shall be installed and maintained unvented fuel heaters are prohibited except for heaters listed for unvented use unvented fuel heaters are prohibited in any bedroom 4 health standards a all premises indoors and out of doors shall be kept free of rodents and vermin b all dwelling units which do not have a central air conditioning system shall have screens on all exterior openable windows and shall have a screen door with a selfclosing device on all exterior doors except for the main entrance door c accessory buildings vacant structures and dwellings or portions thereof shall be kept free from rubbish and garbage d every toilet room bathroom and kitchen floor surface shall be constructed and maintained so as to be substantially impervious to water and so as to permit such floor to be kept in a clean and sanitary condition 5 sanitary facilities a every dwelling unit shall contain at least one kitchen sink one tub or shower one lavatory and one water closet all in good working condition and properly connected to the public water and sewer system all fixtures and piping shall be properly installed and kept free from defects leaks and obstructions b all required plumbing fixtures shall be located within the dwelling unit and be accessible to the occupants of the same the water closet and the tub or shower shall be located in a room affording privacy to the user and shall have a minimum total floor area of 25 square feet c every dwelling unit shall have connected to the kitchen sink lavatory and tub or shower an adequate supply of both cold water and hot water connected to the public water system d every dwelling shall have a water heater properly installed and maintained and capable of heating incoming water to a temperature of 120 degrees fahrenheit and capable of storing not less than 30 gallons of heated water e every dwelling unit shall have garbage disposal facilities or garbage storage containers as specified by chapter 38 6 fire protection a no person shall occupy any dwelling unit which is not in compliance with the city fire prevention code b every dwelling unit shall have at least one approved listed properly installed and maintained smoke detector in good working condition c all cooking lighting and heating equipment shall be installed and maintained in accordance with building electrical mechanical gas and fire prevention codes of the city portable cooking and lighting equipment employing flame is prohibited indoors 7 light and ventilation a every habitable room shall have at least one window which is easily opened and facing directly to the outdoors the minimum total openable window area shall be 57 square feet or eight percent of the total room floor area yearround mechanically ventilated air conditioning systems may be substituted for windows in rooms other than rooms used for sleeping b bathrooms shall comply with the light and ventilation requirements when not equipped with approved exhaust ventilators 8 electric lights and outlets a where there is electric service available to the dwelling every habitable room shall have at least two separate and remote convenience outlets in addition bedrooms shall have at least one wall switch controlled ceiling or wall type light fixture kitchens shall have at least three separate and remote small appliance outlets and at least one wall switch controlled ceiling or wall type light fixture every hall water closet compartment bathroom laundry room room containing furnace and room containing electrical service panel or equipment shall contain at least one electrical light fixture to adequately illuminate equipment and facilities in bathrooms the light fixture shall be controlled by a wall switch every bathroom and laundry room shall contain at least one convenience outlet b all fixtures receptacles equipment and wiring shall be installed and maintained in a state of good repair safe and capable of being used and shall be connected to the available electrical utility source c where the determination is made upon examination of the existing electrical service supply that such electrical service supply is obsolete or is being used in such a manner as would constitute a hazard to the occupants or would otherwise constitute a hazard to life or property a correction shall be in order and the city electrical code shall apply 9 space requirements a each dwelling unit shall contain at least 150 square feet of habitable floor area for the first occupant and at least 90 square feet of additional habitable floor area for each additional occupant b in each dwelling unit of two or more rooms each room occupied for sleeping purposes shall contain at least 64 square feet of floor area for one occupant and an additional 50 square feet of floor area for each additional occupant c children under 12 months of age shall not be considered occupants and onehalf of the area requirements shall apply to children under 12 years of age for purposes of additional occupants in subsection 9a of this section and general occupants in subsection 9b of this section 06     4102018 inspection for the purpose of ascertaining whether violations of this division exist the code enforcement official or any other person authorized by the premises on which the costs were incurred charges may include but are not limited to the expenses of inspection or testing by third parties photography newspaper publication costs title search fees attorney fees costs incurred in identifying locating or contacting the owner mortgagee and lienholders labor and equipment costs for preparation of the premises work to secure repair vacate remove demolish cleanup and removal of debris landfill and waste disposal costs an administrative fee of $10000 or ten percent of the expenses and costs whichever is greater shall be added to the costs b the city council shall certify the expenses incurred in implementing provisions of this division for billing to the owner of the property the bill becomes an account receivable upon completion and shall be due within 30 days c if after 30 days from billing payment in full has not been made the city shall assess the expenses on and have a lien against the property on which the expenses occurred unless it is a homestead as protected by the state constitution d notice of the lien shall be provided to the property owner and the county clerk in a form approved by the city attorney e the citys lien is a privileged lien subordinate only to tax liens and all previously recorded bona fide mortgage liens attached to the real property to which the citys lien attaches such lien shall bear interest at the rate of ten percent per annum until paid f the lien shall be extinguished if the property owner or another person having interest in the legal title to property reimburses the city for the total amount due g this remedy shall be available to the city in addition to any penal or other remedy provided by law or equity which the city state or any other person may have to remedy an unsafe property condition h the city may also direct the city attorney to bring a civil action in a court of competent jurisdiction to collect the amount due plus all associated costs and fees the city attorney is authorized to make use of whatever legal or equitable remedies available to collect the monies due 22   prohibited acts a it shall be unlawful for the owner or occupants of an unsafe condition to fail or refuse to comply with any order of the code enforcement official or the commission panel b it shall be unlawful for any person to obstruct or interfere with the implementation of any action required or permitted by the code enforcement official or commission panel c it shall be unlawful for any person to remove any posted notice including any unsafe structure placard without written permission of the code enforcement official or for any person to enter the structure except for the purpose of making the required inspections repairs or demolishing the same d it shall be unlawful for the owner or occupant of any property to move or relocate any prebuilt building older than ten years for any use except for accessory storage uses e it shall be unlawful for the owner or occupant of any property to move or relocate any manufactured home older than ten years within the city previously owned manufactured homes are subject to inspection by the code enforcement official prior to placement to insure conformance with the minimum standards for housing see section 10114 of the city of yoakum ordinances  1292014   7102018 penalties any person agent firm or corporation who and requirements of the citys electrical and other related codes c conflict of interest the electrical inspector shall not engage in the business of master electrician either directly or indirectly within the city d powers and duties the powers and duties of the electrical inspector and his assistants when so designated by the city manager shall be as follows 1 to have entire supervision over the electrical inspection of all electrical work within the city 2 upon application on proper forms for the installation of electrical wiring devices and equipment and upon payment of the required fees to make inspections of all new electrical installations and make reinspections of any existing electrical installations at such time as he may deem necessary for the purpose of safeguarding of life and property within the city 3 have the right to enter any building during reasonable hours in the discharge of his official duties for the purpose of making any inspection or test of any electrical wiring device and equipment therein where such installations are found dangerous to life or property or to the work of the fire department or otherwise not in conformity with the ordinances of the city he is empowered to disconnect such parts of installations or to order disconnection of electric service to any building after giving notice in writing to the parties concerned and such defective electrical wiring shall not be again connected until made safe as directed by the electrical inspector 4 to decide all disputed questions pertaining to the installation of all electric wiring devices and equipment which shall be interpreted by the electrical inspector by taking into consideration the national electrical in the light of the standards generally recognized by the trade concerning the safe and proper installation of electrical wiring devices and equipment e interference with by others it is unlawful for any person to interfere with the electrical inspector or his assistants in the discharge of their duties or to prevent or in any manner attempt to prevent them from carrying out the provisions of this article 24   gas inspector a position created  duties generally the office of gas inspector is created the city fire marshal or other person designated by the city manager shall perform the duties of such gas inspector he shall have charge supervision and control of all matters rules and regulations pertaining to the installation of natural gas in the city b duty to inspect  no city liability arises by inspection it shall be the duty of the gas inspector to go upon any premises in which the use of natural gas is to be installed and to examine all pipings fittings and connections placed in the buildings and on the premises either by the gas company or by any gas fitter and to see that all rules and regulations have been complied with  but the city shall in no event ever be liable to any person for the manner in which such work of supervision inspection or reinspection is performed by such gas inspector or the authorized agents thereof or for failure to perform such service c right of entry for inspection the gas inspector is codes 00a   membership  vacancies  rules  meetings a regular member panels the building and standards commission shall consist of one or more fivemember panels to be appointed for terms of two years as near as practical members shall be qualified in one or more of the fields of fire prevention building construction sanitation health and public safety b alternate members the city council may appoint eight or more alternate members to serve in the absence of one or more regular members when requested to do so by the city manager the alternate members serve for the same term and are subject to removal in the same manner as regular members a vacancy is filled in the same manner as a vacancy is filled among the regular members c removal  filling vacancies the city council may remove a commission member for cause on a written charge before a decision regarding removal is made the city council must hold a public hearing on the matter if requested by the commission member subject to the removal action a vacancy shall be filled for the unexpired term d rules of order  appointment of officers a majority of the entire commission shall establish rules of order and the appointment of at least a chairperson vicechairperson and secretary and duties thereof the rules of order shall be in compliance with the provisions of this division e meetings  oaths  authority to compel attendance of witnesses meetings of the commission shall be held at the call of the chairperson and at other times as determined by the commission all meetings held by the commission shall be open to the public each chairperson of a panel or in his absence the acting chairperson may administer oaths and compel the attendance of witnesses f minutes and other records the commission shall keep minutes of its proceedings showing the vote of each member on each question or the fact that a member is absent or fails to vote the commission shall keep records of its examinations and other official actions the minutes and records shall be filed immediately in the office of the commission as public records 00be 59102b e f   powers and duties generally the commission is authorized to hold public hearings to determine compliance with or alleged violations of city building and technical codes including minimum property maintenance requirements the commission shall also hear appeals from persons aggrieved by orders or decisions of city officials made in enforcement of this chapter the commission may further make recommendations to the city council as to any needed modifications amendments and changes in this chapter and shall carry out such other duties as may be required from time to time by the city council or state law 00a f   hearing authority and procedure a minimum number of members in review panel all cases heard by the commission may be heard by any panel but at least four members of any panel must hear a case b concurring vote of four members required the concurring vote of four members of the commission is necessary to take any action under this article and any other ordinance under its jurisdiction adopted by the city c official must appear at hearing the code enforcement official shall present all cases initiated by the city to be heard by the commission d evidence testimony and defense there shall be provided ample opportunity at the public hearing for the presentation of evidence or testimony by respondents persons opposing charges and the code enforcement official relating to alleged violations of this chapter e time and method of giving notice of hearing notice of all proceedings before the commission must be given 1 by certified mail return receipt requested to the record owners of the property affected and each holder of a recorded lien against the affected property as shown by the records in the office of the county clerk of the county in which the affected property is located if the address of the lienholder can be ascertained from any applicable instruments on file in the office of the county clerk  2 to all unknown owners by posting a copy of the notice on the front door of each improvement situated on the affected property or as close to the front door as practical  and 3 by publication in a newspaper of general circulation within the city on one occasion the notice shall be mailed published and posted on or before the tenth day before the date of the hearing before the commission and must state the date time and place of the hearing f filing copy of notice in official real property records the commission may file notice of a proceeding before a commission panel in the official public records of real property in the county in which the affected property is located the notice must contain the name and address of the owner of the affected property if that information can be determined from a reasonable search of the instruments on file at the office of the county clerk a legal description of the affected property and a description of the proceeding the filing of the notice is binding on subsequent grantees lienholders or other transferees of an interest in property who acquire such interest after the filing of the notice and constitutes notice of the proceeding on any subsequent recipient of any interest who acquires such interest after the filing of the notice g final determination by commission the commission may 1 declare a structure or premises substandard dangerous or otherwise in violation of this chapter 2 order an unsafe condition be abated vacated secured repaired removed or demolished within a fixed period 3 order in appropriate cases the immediate abatement vacation securing repairing removal or demolition of the unsafe condition the entry onto private property to secure such abatement if it is determined that conditions exist on the property that constitutes a violation of this article or any other ordinance within its jurisdiction and order action to be taken as necessary to remedy alleviate or remove any unsafe structure found to exist 4 issue orders or directives to any peace officer of the state including a sheriff or constable or the chief of police of the city to enforce and carry out the lawful orders or directives of the panel 5 determine the amount and duration of the civil penalty the city may recover as provided in this article h notice of final determination the commission shall 1 promptly send by first class mail certified return receipt requested a copy of any final decision and order to all persons to whom notice is required to be sent under this section  and 2 publish an abbreviated copy of the order one time in a newspaper of general circulation in the city within ten calendar days after the date of the mailing of the copy as required in this section including street address or the legal description of the property the date of hearing a brief statement indicating the results of the order and instructions stating where a complete copy of the order may be obtained a copy shall be filed in the office of the city clerk i effect of final determination  civil penalties a determination made under this article is binding and constitutes prima facie evidence of the penalty in any court of competent jurisdiction in a civil suit brought by the city for final judgment in accordance with the established penalty to enforce any civil penalty under this article the city clerk must file with the district clerk of the county in which the city is located a certified copy of the order of the commission panel establishing the amount and duration of the penalty no other proof is required for a district court to enter final judgment on the penalty if no appeals are taken from the decision of the commission panel within the required period the decision of the commission panel is in all things final and binding j rehearing and reconsideration  stay of proceedings any owner lienholder or mortgagee of record jointly or severally aggrieved by any decision or order of a commission panel may request a single rehearing of the case by a second existing duly appointed commission panel or if no such panel exists the same may request reconsideration from the first panel the request must be in writing addressed to the commission specifying the grounds for the request and received by the commission or postmarked on or before the tenth day after the mailing of the notice required under this article the rehearing or reconsideration panel shall consider the grounds for the request for rehearing or reconsideration and may approve or deny the request only the approval of the request for rehearing or reconsideration stays all other proceedings k appeal after a final decision of the commission under this article any owner lienholder or mortgagee of record remaining jointly or severally aggrieved by the final decision of the commission may appeal the decision to a court of competent jurisdiction in accordance with secs 1018610208  reserved division 3  construction board of adjustments and appeals definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this division shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning builder means one that builds who contracts for and supervises the construction of buildings building industry representative means one who sells building supplies means the citys building plumbing electrical and mechanical code enforcement officer or one charged with enforcement of codes or ordinances contractor means one that provides materials and services at a specified price for the construction of buildings design professional means a registered professional engineer or architect health or medical professional means the citys appointed health officer medical doctor dentist or physicians assistant legal professional means an attorney   i 2 5141996 established the city has established a construction board of adjustments and appeals which consists of seven members and two alternates the board shall be appointed by the city council   ii 5141996 membership officers meetings and rules of procedure a regular members the board shall consist of seven members composed of to the extent possible individuals with knowledge and experience regarding the city building code plumbing code electrical code mechanical code and backflow prevention and crossconnection control the membership should also include to the extent possible design professionals contractors builders legal professionals and health or medical professionals b alternate members in addition to the regular members there should be two alternate members one member at large from the building industry and one member at large from the public c conflict of interest no board member shall act in a case in which he has a personal or financial interest d terms the terms of office of the board members shall be staggered so that no more than onethird of the board is appointed or replaced in any 12month period the two alternates if appointed shall serve oneyear terms e vacancies vacancies shall be filled for an unexpired term in the manner in which original appointments are required to be made f removal from office for failure to attend meetings continued absence of any member from required meetings of the board shall at the discretion of the applicable governing body render any such member subject to immediate removal from office g quorum and voting a simple majority of the board shall constitute a quorum in varying any provision of this article the affirmative votes of the majority present but not less than three affirmative votes shall be required in modifying a decision of the code official not less than four affirmative votes but not less than a majority of the board shall be required in the event that regular members are unable to attend a meeting the alternate members if appointed shall vote h officers the board members shall elect from its membership a chairperson vicechairperson and secretary the election shall be held at the first meeting following the annual term appointments the secretary of the board shall make a detailed record of all of its proceedings which shall set forth the reasons for its decision the vote of each member the absence of a member and any failure of a member to vote i procedural rules and regulations the board shall establish rules and regulations for its own procedure not inconsistent with the provisions of this article j meetings the board shall meet on call of the chairperson the board shall meet within 30 calendar days after notice of appeal has been received k powers and duties generally the board shall have the authority to hear appeals of decisions and interpretations of the code official and consider variances of the technical building plumbing electric and mechanical codes including backflow prevention and crossconnection control regulations in the manner provided in this article and by state law  5125 5127a  iii iv 5141996 matters that may be appealed to the board the owner of a building structure or service system or his duly authorized agent may appeal a decision of the code official to the construction board of adjustments and appeals whenever any one of the following conditions are claimed to exist 1 the code official rejected or refused to approve the mode or manner of construction proposed to be followed or materials to be used in the installation or alteration of a building structure or service system 2 the provisions of the applicable code or ordinance do not apply to the specific case 3 that an equally good or more desirable form of installation can be employed in any specific case 4 the true intent and meaning of the applicable code or ordinance or any of the regulations thereunder have been misconstrued or incorrectly interpreted a  v 5141996 notice of appeal to board a form and time for filing notice of appeal to the board shall be in writing addressed to the board and filed within 30 calendar days after the decision is rendered by the code official appeals shall be in a form acceptable to the board b time for appeal may be shortened for unsafe or dangerous buildings or service systems in the case of a building structure or service system which in the opinion of the code official is unsafe unsanitary or dangerous the code official may in his order limit the time for such appeals to a shorter period d  v 5141996 authority of board to grant variances a required findings the construction board of adjustments and appeals when so appealed to and after a hearing may vary the application of any provision of the applicable code or ordinance to any particular case when in its opinion the enforcement thereof would do manifest injustice and would be contrary to the spirit and purpose of this or the technical codes or public interest and also finds that 1 special conditions and circumstances exist which are peculiar to the building structure or service system involved and which are not applicable to others  2 the special conditions and circumstances do not result from the action or inaction of the applicant  3 granting the variance requested will not confer on the applicant any special privilege that is denied by the applicable code or ordinance to other buildings structures or service system  4 the variance granted is the minimum variance that will make possible the reasonable use of the building structure or service system  and 5 the grant of the variance will be in harmony with the general intent and purpose of the applicable code or ordinance and will not be detrimental to the public health safety and general welfare and shall be in conformance with state and federal requirements b conditional variances in granting the variance the board may prescribe a reasonable time limit within which the action for which the variance is required shall be commenced or completed or both in addition the board may prescribe appropriate conditions and safeguards in conformity with the applicable code or ordinance violation of the conditions of a variance shall be deemed a violation of the applicable code or ordinance b c  v 5141996 final decisions a to be entered without delay the board shall in every case reach a decision without unreasonable or unnecessary delay b reasons for decision to be included each decision of the board shall include the reasons for the decision c duty of city official to comply with decision if a decision of the board reverses or modifies a refusal order or disallowance of the code official or varies the application of any provision of this article the code official shall immediately take action in accordance with such decision d decision to be filed in the office of the code official every decision shall be promptly filed in writing in the office of the code official and shall be open to public inspection e notice to parties and public a certified copy of the decision shall be sent by mail or otherwise to the appellant and a copy shall be kept publicly posted in the office of the code official for two weeks after filing f decisions final subject to remedies at law or in equity every decision of the board shall be final subject however to such remedy as any aggrieved party might have at law or in equity b  vi 5141996 role of city council regarding questions of interpretation and enforcement a it is the intent of this chapter that all questions of interpretation and enforcement shall be first presented to the administrative official and that such questions shall be presented to the board of adjustments only on appeal from the decision of the city inspector and that recourse from the decisions of the board of adjustments shall be to the courts as provided by state law b it is further the intent of this chapter that the duties of the city council in connection with this chapter shall not include hearing and deciding questions of interpretation and enforcement that may arise the procedure for deciding such questions shall be as provided in this article under this chapter the city council shall have only the duties of considering and adopting or rejecting proposed amendments or the repeal of this chapter as provided by law and establishing fees as provided in this article  1101989 secs 1021710232  reserved article iv  examination and licensing of electricians examining and supervising board of electricians created  membership there is created a board for the examination of electricians within the city to be known as the examining and supervising board of electricians the board shall consist of five members one member shall be the fire marshal of the city one member shall be the electrical superintendent two members shall be master electricians licensed and bonded with the city and one shall be a citizen at large member the members of the board shall be appointed by the mayor subject to the approval by the city council the members of such board shall continue to act as the examining and supervising board of electricians until their successors have been appointed and such appointments approved by the city council if for any reason a vacancy is created on the board the mayor shall appoint a new member such appointment shall not become effective until approved by the city council    compensation members of the examining and supervising board of electricians shall receive no compensation for their services on the board other than the fees which may be allowed them by the city council for conducting examinations of applicants for licenses    conducting examinations waiving a the board created above may fix dates at reasonable times for having applications for examinations for licenses and may pass upon all persons engaged in the electrical business as master electricians journeyman electricians and maintenance electricians b a nonrefundable fee shall be assessed on all applicants license the fee for a masters examination or a journeyman and maintenance examination shall be as set from time to time by the city council in the manual of fees and service charges of the city c the examining and supervising board of electricians may waive the requirements of an examination upon presentation to the board of evidence of experience and education which clearly shows the applicants qualification for the type of license for which applied the board shall have the complete control in establishing qualifications required for the type of license for which applied such licenses may be renewable nonrenewable or designated for specific projects    issuance of license a whenever an applicant successfully meets the requirements prescribed by the board the board shall issue a license to such person and shall record the issuance of such license in a book to be kept for such purpose no license shall be issued to a master electrician until the required bond is filed and license fee paid an electricians license shall not be issued to any previous holder of one which has been revoked except upon a new application approved by the examining board b for the purpose of this article a valid electricians license issued by the state meets all of the requirements of a cityissued electricians license herein and is accepted in lieu of such cityissued license and entitles such license holder to do work within the scope of the electrical license in accordance with all electrical codes and regulations of the city      382005 license period renewal authorized all renewable licenses expire on each december 31 such licenses must be renewed each year prior to expiration holders of licenses which have expired must apply for new licensing in the same manner as new license applicants    license not transferable illegal use of licensees name no license shall be transferable and no holder thereof shall allow his name to be used by any other party either for the purpose of doing work or obtaining a permit under penalty of forfeiture of his license and punishment as provided in section 115    scope of master electricians license a master electricians license shall entitle the holder thereof to engage in the business of installing wiring and electrical apparatus inside or on any building for use in connection with electric light heat or power within the city and installing wiring and electrical apparatus inside or on any building for use in connection with electric light heat or power outside the city if the property is served by the municipal electric system    suspension and revocation of license the electrical inspector shall have the right and authority to suspend the license of any electrician upon the violation of any portion of this chapter and the electrical inspector shall upon suspension file with the city clerk a statement setting forth the reasons for such suspension a copy of such report to be filed with the clerk to be delivered to the electrician any electrician aggrieved by such suspension may file a written appeal to city council within ten days of receipt of suspension notice presentation and consideration of the appeal shall be presented to city council at their next regular scheduled meeting the city council may affirm or rescind such suspension or revoke the license and order the forfeiture of a master electrician bond in the event that the master electrician whose license has been suspended fails or refuses to appeal to the city council within ten days from the date of such suspension the city clerk shall place before the city council the report of the electrical inspector at the next regular meeting for action by the city council to revoke the suspension or to revoke the license and forfeit the bond as herein provided    businesses footnotes  1  state law reference municipal regulation of miscellaneous businesses vtca
