manner as is required under this article for the drilling of any other well d a relief well permit will be for a sixmonth period only and any relief well not completed as a producing well shall be plugged and abandoned within six months after commencement of drilling operations unless an extension is granted by the city council art ii  16 6101980 secs 30383062  reserved article iii  unitization purpose to facilitate the orderly development of oil and gas production in the city and to avoid confiscation of property all mineral interests in each unit for which a permit is granted shall be unitized as provided in this article art iv  1 6101980 well density restrictions no more than one completion shall be made in any reservoir on any unit until special field rules have been adopted by the railroad commission for the reservoir the final well density within each unit shall be no greater than that prescribed by the railroad commission in special field rules which may be adopted for the field art iv  1 6101980 procedure a not exclusive the procedure provided in this section for the unitization of oil and gas interests is not intended to be an exclusive method for unitizing the interests voluntary unitization is authorized as a substitute for the procedures provided in this section b options in the event an application for permit for the drilling completion and operation of an oil or gas well is made by a person who does not own in fee or hold by lease or drilling contract from the owners all of the operating rights in the unit as to which the permit is granted then all of the owners of the operating rights not held or controlled by the permittee shall be entitled to the following options 1 mineral fee owners a mineral fee owner of an oil and gas interest not covered by an existing oil and gas lease shall be entitled to participate as a royalty owner on the basis of onesixth royalty interest in the property covered by his mineral fee in addition the mineral fee owner shall be entitled to elect between the options available to the lessees in this section  however if the mineral fee owner fails to elect between the options available to the lessee within 30 days after the giving of the notice provided for this section he shall be conclusively presumed to have elected to participate as a royalty owner on the basis of a onesixth royalty if any mineral fee owner owns an interest in the oil and gas on in and under the land less than the entire fee simple oil and gas mineral estate then the royalty participation of the mineral fee owner and his share of participation as an operating owner or as a carried owner under options no 1 or 2 below shall be reduced in the proportion that his interest bears to the whole and undivided fee and in accordance with the nature of the estate of which he is seized 2 oil and gas lessees an oil and gas lessee shall be entitled to elect between the following options a option no 1 lessee may elect within 30 days after the date of posting of the notice to participate in the drilling and production of the well as an active operating interest owner in which event he shall pay his proportionate part of all drilling and operating costs and shall participate in production in proportion to his ownership in the production unit if the owner elects to participate as an operation owner he shall either post bond written by a good and sufficient corporate surety company or deposit cash with the permittee guaranteeing payment to the permittee of the operating interest owners proportionate share on a surface acreage basis of the following amounts the estimated monthly operating expenses if the cost of drilling and completing the well exceeds the estimated cost the owner shall forthwith on demand pay his proportionate share of the excess to the permittee or if the actual costs are less than the estimate the owners proportionate share of the difference shall be refunded by permittee on demand such operating interest owner shall advance to applicant at monthly or other mutually acceptable intervals the owners share of estimate expenses of operating the production unit or at the election of the permittee the owners share of the operating expenses may be deducted by permittee as they accrue from the revenues from production which otherwise would be payable to the owner b option no 2 lessee may elect to become the owner of a carried interest if lessee elects to be a carried interest owner he shall not be entitled to receive any revenue from his interest in the drilling block until the time as the participating owners have received from the proceeds of production attributable to the carried interest owners leasehold interest an amount equal to his proportionate part of the current operating expenses the cost of purchasing and installing all pipeline tank batteries and other equipment installed by the participating owners to facilitate production of oil and gas from the drilling block and an amount equal to the carried interest owners proportionate share of the cost of drilling and completing the well within the unit the interest of the carried interest owner shall be subject to its proportionate share of the unit in accordance with accepted accounting procedures any remaining income attributable to the carried interest shall be payable to the owner thereof monthly if a lessee fails to elect to participate under one of the two options shown herein within 30 days after the date of notice given to him as hereinafter provided then and in that event the lessee shall be presumed to have elected to participate as a carried interest owner under option no 2 c notice to owners notice to the owners whose addresses are known or are ascertainable to use of ordinary diligence of the oil and gas interests within the affected unit that are not owned or leased by the permittee and that are not covered by voluntary unitization agreements shall be given as follows 1 the permittee shall deliver or send by certified mail to all the owners at their last known address a written notice in the form approved by the city council a copy of which is available in the office of the city clerk the notice shall include a a legal description of the unit b the type of interest held by the owner being notified mineral fee royalty lessee overriding royalty etc c a statement of the options available to the owner being notified as set out in this section if applicable d notification that if the owner fails to notify the applicant in writing within 30 days from the date of mailing or delivering the notice to the owner of the selection of one of the available options the owner will be conclusively presumed to have elected to participate as a royalty owner in the case of a fee owner and as a carried interest owner in the case of a lessee 2 in addition to the individual notification the applicant shall publish in two issues of a newspaper of general circulation in the city a notice in substantial compliance with the form approved by the city council and available in the office of the city clerk art iv  2 6101980 allocation of production  agreements for alternative allocation a production from any unit shall be allocated to tracts that are unitized under the provisions of this article in the proportion that the number of surface square feet of each the individual tract has to the total surface square footage in the unit owners of interests under the tracts shall share in the production allocated to the individual tracts on the basis of their respective interests therein production from the unit in which the owner participates shall be treated as production from all of the tracts within the unit b the permittee and the owners of other mineral interests in any unit may alter the obligations set out in this article by agreement between them provided that the agreement is not in conflict with the other provisions of this article art iv  3 6101980 secs 30673090  reserved article iv  drilling and operational standards and specifications earthen and steel pits it is unlawful for any person to use in connection with any drilling or reworking operation within the city any earthen pit all pits shall be portable steel pits which shall be removed from the city with their contents promptly upon the completion or abandonment of the well art ii  1 6101980 crude oil storage and receiving tanks after any oil or gas well is brought into production all crude oil storage or receiving tanks for the well must be located outside the city limits art ii  2 6101980 derricks and rigs no operator shall use or operate in connection with the drilling or reworking of any well any wooden derrick or steam powered rig motive power for all drilling and other operations shall be diesel electric or gas or gasoline engines all engines shall be equipped with effective mufflers no steampowered rig shall be permitted no drilling rig or derrick shall be permitted to remain on the drilling site for a period of longer than 30 days after the completion or abandonment of the well art ii  3 6101980 drilling fluid the bore holes of all wells while being drilled or reworked shall at all times contain drilling fluid of sufficient weight to exceed the formation pressure anticipated and of the weight and viscosity a reasonably prudent operator would use to keep the well under control art ii  4 6101980 blowout preventers a two dual controlled fluid operated blowout preventers with working pressure rating equal to the maximum anticipated wellhead pressure shall be used for all drilling or completion operations involving the use of drill pipe or tubing after the surface casing has been set a hydril type blowout preventer shall be used in addition to the two dual controlled blowout preventers above specified a choke manifold having the same working pressure rating as the preventers shall be installed below the blowout preventer stack b the mechanical operation of the blow out preventers shall be checked a minimum of every 24 hours and pressure tested prior to installation on each casing string art ii  5 6101980 drill stem tests no drill stem test shall be conducted except during daylight hours and then only if the well effluent during the test is produced adequate oil and gas separator to storage tanks and the effluent remaining in the drill pipe at the time the tool is closed is flushed to the surface by circulating drilling fluid down the annulus and up the drill pipe art ii  6 6101980 surface casing a all operators shall be required to set and cement a sufficient amount of surface casing to protect properly all fresh water sands in accordance with the requirements of any governmental agency having jurisdiction the surface casing shall however in no case be set to a depth of less than 1150 feet b the surface casing shall be of new casing and shall be cemented by the pump and plug method c a volume of cement shall be used that according to accepted engineering procedures is calculated to fill the annular space between the surface casing and well bore to the surface of the ground and the cement shall be allowed to stand for a minimum period of 12 hours under pressure and for 24 hours before drilling plug or initiating test d after cementing the surface casing shall be tested by pump pressure of at least 750 pounds per square inch if at the end of 30 minutes the pressure shows a drop of 150 pounds per square inch or more the casing shall be condemned after corrective operations the casing shall again be tested in the same manner art ii  7 6101980 production and protection casing the producing or protection strings of casing shall be of new pipe meeting api specifications cementing shall be by the pump and plug method and a volume of cement which is according to accepted engineering standards sufficient to fill the annular space between the casing and the well bore to a point at least 600 feet above the shoe or the highest producing zone whichever is the shallower depth cement shall be allowed to stand for a minimum period of 12 hours before drilling the plug art ii  8 6101980 formation pressures no well shall be completed or operated in a zone which is reasonably anticipated to produce shutin pressures in excess of the working pressure rating of the standard api wellhead equipment on the well art ii  9 6101980 wellheads all wells drilled or completed in the city shall be equipped with casing heads tubing heads and wellhead connections conforming to api standards the casing heads on the wells shall have working pressure ratings of not less than 3000 pounds per square inch tubing heads and wellhead connections used on the wells shall have working pressure ratings in excess of the wells shutin surface pressure all the wells having a surface shutin pressure of 3000 pounds per square inch or less shall be equipped with at least one master valve and one wing valve all wells having surface shutin pressures in excess of 3000 pounds per square inch shall be equipped with at least two master valves and one wing valve and no such well shall have threaded connections between the surface safety valve and the christmas tree art ii  10 6101980 multiple and tubingless completions multiple completions and tubingless completions are permitted art ii  11 6101980 surface safety valves a highlow surface safety valve shall be installed on all wells with a surface shutin pressure in excess of 3000 pounds per square inch art ii  12 6101980 subsurface safety valves all flowing wells having shutin well head pressure of 1500 pounds per square inch or above or which are located within 50 feet of a public street shall be equipped with subsurface safety valve installed in the tubing or production string the valve shall be pulled and inspected each year between april 1 and august 1 and more often if desired by the operator and a report of the inspection shall be filed with the city clerk art ii  13 6101980 fences all wells and production facilities shall be adequately protected by a sixfoot chainlink fence with a barbed wire guard at the top and a gate with heavy duty lock art ii  18 6101980 pumping unit prime movers only electric prime movers shall be permitted for the purpose of pumping wells art ii  19 6101980 vented gas no operator shall allow gas to escape or be vented into the air except for bleed gas normally vented from standard gas operated controls and normal stock tank vapors all gas burned shall be burned in a manner which does not create or constitute a fire hazard and the location of the torch pipe or other burning device the construction thereof the maintenance and operation thereof shall at all times be in compliance with the regulations as may be from time to time issued by the city fire department art ii  20 6101980 salt water and waste disposal all salt water produced from any oil or gas well shall be disposed of outside the confines of the city limits no person shall permit any crude oil gas or other petroleum product salt water mud or other effluent to spill over overflow leak drain out escape or accumulate in or about the premises on any surface in any open surface ditch or other exposed surface conduit or any sewer no person shall handle any hydrocarbon in any manner or amount which creates a potential fire hazard or permit any condition which may pollute any surface or subsurface water or damage any publiclyowned land art ii  21 6101980 electrical insulation and isolation all wells must be electrically isolated from all metallic piping and gathering systems unless the well and the piping are cathodically protected as a system electrical isolation of the wells shall be by the use of insulating sleeves and washers in flanges or insulating unions the effectiveness of the insulating devices must be tested at least every six months and the results of the test reported to the city clerk art ii  22 6101980 maintenance of premises and surface equipment all surface areas utilized by an operator for production facilities shall be kept clear of high grass weeds and combustible trash and other rubbish or debris  all surface equipment shall be maintained in good condition art ii  23 6101980 fire hazard and well and operation identification signs printed signs with at least two inch letters reading danger no smoking or open flames allowed or similar words shall be posted in conspicuous places on each well and production facility the signs shall include the drilling block number and the emergency telephone number of the fire department well and lease designations required by the railroad commission or any other governmental authority having jurisdiction shall also be displayed art ii  23 6101980 blocking of streets and alleys except when necessary to protect life or property in connection with emergency operations no street or alley shall be blocked or obstructed by any drilling or producing operations unless prior consent for the blockage is obtained in the form of a resolution by the city council art ii  24 6101980 electrical storms and hurricanes no well shall be permitted to produce at any time during an electrical storm or hurricane all drilling and reworking operations shall be shut down during any hurricane and drill pipe shall be either laid down or left in the well bore and drilling and workover masts shall be laid down art ii  25 6101980 pipelines excavation for and installation of pipeline to move oil and gas from any well site across city rightsofway should be as provided in section 401 art ii  17 6101980 loss of control of well a in the event of the loss of control of any well the operator shall immediately take all reasonable steps to regain control of the well regardless of any other provisions of this article and shall notify the city oil and gas inspector as soon as practicable after receipt of notice by the operator of the occurrence of the loss of well control endangering persons or property b if the city oil and gas inspector certifies in writing to the city clerk that in his opinion danger to persons or property exists because of the loss or well control briefly describing the same and the operator is not taking or is unable to take all reasonably necessary steps to regain control of the well the city oil and gas inspector may employ any well control experts or other contractors or suppliers of special services or may incur any other expenses for labor or material that the city oil and gas inspector deems necessary to regain control of the well c the city shall have a valid lien against the interest owners in the well to secure the payment of any expenditures made by the city pursuant to any the action in regaining control of the well however the lien shall attach to the interest in the well of those persons who have been presumed to have elected to participate as carried interest owners under this article art ii  15 6101980 parks and recreation footnotes  1  state law reference municipal parks and other recreational and cultural resources generally vtca local the affairs of the city the parks superintendent may choose to have the parks and recreation board make a final determination on the application b fees the parks and recreation board may establish occupant of any corner lot in the city to place maintain or permit or cause to be placed or maintained any plant having a height greater than three feet above the level of the center of the nearest abutting street or in that area which lies between the property line of such corner lot and the curblines of streets abutting such property lines and which area extends for a distance of 50 feet back from the intersection of the curblines of such abutting streets d the invalidity of any section or provision of this section shall not invalidate other sections or provisions thereof  1822  a 3a 1161957  i 4142015 tree or other plant between property line and curbline it is unlawful for either the owner or the occupant of any lot in the city to place maintain or permit or cause to be placed or maintained any tree or other plant on or in the area between the property line thereof and the curbline of any street abutting such property line in such a way as to obstruct the free passage on and use of that area by the public   b 1161957 tree or other plant near fire hydrant it is unlawful for either the owner or occupant of any property in the city to place maintain or permit or cause to be placed or maintained thereon any tree or other plant within five feet of any fire hydrant in the city   c 1161957 minimum vegetation height above street  pruning required it is unlawful for the owner or occupant of any property in the city to maintain or permit limbs of trees growing thereon to overhang or grow above the area between the property line and the curbline of any abutting street unless such limbs and all branches and foliage thereon are kept trimmed and pruned to a minimum of eight feet above the street level at the nearest curbline   d 1161957 enforcement a authority of city inspector to identify visibility obstructions obstruction of visibility at an intersection and other violations of this division shall be determined by the city inspector b appeal of inspectors determination any person who does not agree with the decision of the city inspector shall have an appeal to the zoning board of adjustments and appeals if the board determines that there is no obstruction of visibility or other violation the person shall not be required to remove any fences walls or hedges or remove or trim vegetation as required in this division if the board determines that there is an obstruction the party shall be considered in violation of this section and subject to charges being filed in municipal court unless the object is immediately removed c duty of chief of police to serve notice of violation it shall be the duty of the chief of police to cause a written notice to be served upon the owner or occupant of any property upon which there exists a violation of this division the notice shall advise the owner or occupant of the nature of the violation and that the violation must be corrected within ten days after serving of the notice the notice shall further advise the owner or occupant that if such condition is not corrected or remedied within the tenday period the city manager may cause the violation to be removed or corrected at the owners expense d failure of owner to correct violations the owner or occupant of any property who shall fail within ten days after service of such written notice by the chief of police to trim prune or remove any such tree plant hedge wall fence or other structure or vegetation that violates the provisions of this division shall be deemed guilty of a misdemeanor and upon conviction thereof shall be punished as provided in section 115 a separate offense shall be deemed to have been committed on every day that any such violation is permitted to remain after the expiration of the period of ten days after the service of the notice the property owner shall also be responsible for all costs of correction of the violation e authority of city manager to trim or remove vegetation the city manager is authorized to remove or cause to be removed any tree or plants found between the opposite curblines in any street in the city and to trim branches limbs or foliage of any tree or plant which overhangs or grows above the area which lies between the opposite curblines of any street so as to provide a minimum clearance of eight feet above the street level at the curbline and so as to be graduated toward the center of the street to a clearance of 12 feet above the street level at the center of the street  18271829  b 3e 3f 4a 1161957   secs 40774095  reserved article iii  sidewalks obstruction prohibited it is unlawful for any person to place or cause to be placed or allow to remain on any street or sidewalk in the city any box barrel crate merchandise fuel or any other article which in any way obstructs the free passage along such street or sidewalk  provided however this section shall not apply to merchandise or other articles on sidewalks which are actually being received or sent out if the same do not occupy more than half of the sidewalk and do not remain thereon for more than one hour    1091925 uniform width and specified grade required in business districts in the business districts sidewalk construction shall be of a uniform width of ten feet and on the grade established by the city engineer    331913 crosswalks to be constructed by property owners when the city constructs crosswalks over the streets or roadways of the city it shall be the duty of the abutting property owner to construct a crosswalk of like character as his sidewalk to connect such sidewalk at the curbline with the crosswalk constructed by the city    331913 subdivisions footnotes  1  state law reference municipal and county authority to regulate subdivisions vtca local government et seq seq article i  in general definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this chapter shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning approved plat means a plat of a subdivision which has been approved in accordance with the requirements of this chapter and regulations and which has been filed for record with the county clerks of dewitt or lavaca counties in instances where a lot lies in both counties the approved plat must be filed in both counties easement means a right granted for the purpose of limited public or semipublic use across over or under private land lot means land occupied or to be occupied by a building and its accessory buildings and including such open spaces as are required by ordinances of the city and having its principal frontage upon a public street or officially approved place lot of record means a lot which is part of a subdivision the plat of which has been recorded in the offices of the county clerks of dewitt or lavaca counties or parcel of land the deed for which was recorded in the offices of the county clerks of dewitt or lavaca counties prior to the passage of the ordinance from which this chapter is derived plat means a complete and exact subdivision plan submitted to the city council for final approval and which if approved will be submitted to the county clerks of dewitt or lavaca counties standards means the official maps comprehensive master plans ordinances and specifications of the city street means a way for vehicular traffic whether designated a street highway thoroughfare parkway throughway road avenue boulevard alley land place or however otherwise designated including 1 street primary or arterial means a street used primarily for fast or heavy traffic designated in the major street plan as a primary street expressway or freeway 2 street secondary or collector means a street that carries traffic from minor streets to the major system of arterial streets and highways including the principal entrance streets of a residential development and streets for circulation within such a development designated in the major street plan as secondary streets 3 street minor means a street used primarily for access to abutting properties 4 street marginal means a minor street that is parallel to and adjacent to arterial streets and highways and that provides access to abutting properties and protection from 5 street culdesac means a short minor street having but one vehicular service access to another street and terminated by vehicular turnarounds 6 street deadend means a street other than a culdesac with only one outlet 7 alley means a minor way used primarily for vehicular service access to the back or the side of properties otherwise abutting on a street subdivider and developer are synonymous and include any person partnership firm association corporation or any officer agent employee servant and trustee thereof who does or participates in the doing of any act toward the subdivision of land within the intent scope and purview of this chapter subdivision means the division of a parcel of land into two or more lots or tracts for the purpose of transfer of ownership dedication of streets alleys or easements or for use for building development  provided a division of land for agricultural purposes into lots or tracts of five acres or more and not involving a new street or alley shall not be deemed a subdivision the term subdivision includes resubdivision and when appropriate to the context shall relate to the process of subdividing or to the land subdivided    art ii 981971 purpose and intent the purpose and intent of this chapter is to provide procedure and standards for the development layout and design of subdivisions of land within the city and for such other areas as may be authorized by state law and to 1 promote and develop the utilization of land to ensure the best possible community environment in accordance with the master plan of the city 2 guide and assist and expedite the developers in correct procedures to be followed and to inform them of the standards which shall be required 3 protect the public interest by controlling the location design class and type of streets sidewalks utilities and essential areas and services required 4 protect and promote the health safety and general welfare    art i 981971 minimum standards in the interpretation and application of the provisions of these regulations it is the intention of the city council that the principles standards and requirements provided for herein shall be minimum requirements for the platting and developing of subdivisions in the city and where other provisions of this more restrictive in their requirements such other provisions shall control    art i 981971 fees all fees related to this chapter shall be established from time to time by the council as provided in the city fee schedule fees shall be collected by the city in advance and no action of the city council shall be valid until the applicable fees have been paid to the city these fees shall be charged on all plats regardless of the action taken by the city council whether the plat is approved or denied the money collected shall defray the cost of administrative clerical and inspection services necessary to properly investigate the plats replats and subdivisions    art vii 981971 variances a the city council may authorize a variance from these regulations when in its opinion undue hardship will result from requiring strict compliance in granting a variance the city council shall prescribe only conditions that it deems necessary or desirable to the public interest in making the findings required in this section b in determining whether to grant a variance the city council shall take into account the nature of the proposed use of land involved and existing uses of the land in the vicinity the number of persons who will reside or work in the proposed subdivision and the probable effect of such variances upon traffic conditions and upon the public health safety convenience and welfare in the vicinity no variance will be granted unless the city council finds that 1 there are special circumstances or conditions affecting the land involved such that the strict application of the provisions of this chapter would deprive the applicant of the reasonable use of his land 2 the variance is necessary for the preservation and enjoyment of a substantial property right of the applicant that the granting of the variance will not be detrimental to the public health safety or welfare or injurious to other property in the area 3 the granting of the variance will not have the effect of preventing the orderly subdivision of other lands in the area in accordance with the provisions of this chapter c such findings of the city council together with the specific facts on which such findings are based shall be incorporated under the official minutes of the city council meeting at which such variance is granted d variances may be granted only when in harmony with the general purpose and intent of this chapter so that the public health safety and welfare may be secured and substantial justice done pecuniary hardship to the subdivider standing alone shall not be deemed to constitute undue hardship the city council may not authorize a variance that would constitute a violation of any other valid ordinance of the city    art x 981971 violations declared public nuisance  enforcement authority of city manager any subdivision of land being developed in violation of the terms and provisions of these regulations is declared to be a public nuisance and the city manager is authorized to institute any action which may be necessary to restrain or abate such violation    981971 withholding city services and facilities for noncompliance a the city defines its policy to be that the city will withhold all city improvements and facilities of whatsoever nature including the maintenance of streets and the furnishing of sewerage facilities and water services from all additions the platting of which has not been approved by the city planning commission b the city may withhold the issuing of a street number or building permit for the erection of any building in the city on a newly subdivided parcel of land until all the requirements of these subdivision regulations have been complied with including installation of and acceptance by the city of all waterworks sewerage and paving improvements for the area designated c no construction work shall begin on the proposed improvements in any proposed subdivision prior to approval of the final plat by the city and the filing of such plat with the county clerks of the dewitt or lavaca counties  art vid 981971 secs 4284232  reserved article ii  plat procedure preapplication consultation the subdivider shall avail himself of the advice and assistance of the city manager before preparing the preliminary plat and before formal application for its approval in order to save time and money and to make the most of his opportunities    art iiia 981971 preliminary plat submission and review a application filing on reaching conclusions informally as recommended above regarding the general program and objectives the subdivider shall prepare a preliminary plat together with improvement plans and other supplementary material as applicable in other sections of this article five copies of the preliminary plat and supplementary materials specified shall be submitted to the city with the filing fee as provided in the city fee schedule and written application for conditional approval at least ten days prior to the city council meeting at which it is to be considered b size  scale  paper all preliminary plats shall be printed on good grade processed paper blue line or direct black and white copies or prints of the proposed subdivision shall be drawn on sheets a maximum size of 24 inches by 36 inches and drawn to a scale of 90 feet to the inch one inch equals 90 feet in cases of large developments which would exceed the dimensions of the sheet of 90 foot scale the preliminary plat may be at a scale of 200 feet to the inch one inch equals 200 feet each subdivision consisting of three acres or more shall be prepared on a topographic base map showing contours at intervals not greater than five feet any subdivision smaller than three acres which in the opinion of the city manager would be affected by the topographical features of the terrain shall also show contours at two foot intervals all topographical maps shall be based on sea level data c content the application for proposed subdivision shall show the following 1 the title of the subdivision or addition name of subdividers and engineer surveyor or planner platting the tract 2 boundary lines bearings and distances sufficient to locate the exact area proposed for subdivision 3 the name and location of all adjoining subdivisions shall be drawn to the same scale and shown in dotted lines adjacent to the tract proposed for subdivision in sufficient detail to show accurately the existing streets and alleys and other features that may influence the layout of development of the proposed subdivision adjacent unplatted land shall be so designated if there is no adjacent subdivision then a map on a smaller scale must be presented to show the nearest subdivision and how the streets alleys or highways in the subdivision submitted may connect with those in the nearest subdivision 4 recorded lot lines survey abstract lines corporation lines and the location of existing utility easements streets highways expressways and freeways traversing abutting or within a reasonable distance 5 the proposed locations and widths of streets alleys easements walkways open channels and lots 6 the location of all existing property lines buildings sewer or water mains gas mains or other underground structures easements or other existing features within the area proposed for subdivision 7 lot or tract numbers or city block numbers addition names and dates recorded 8 proposed arrangement of lots and proposed use of same  however approval of a preliminary plat or final plat with uses so indicated does not constitute approval of such uses 9 proposed building lines showing conformance with this article and city zoning regulations 10 the title under which the proposed subdivision is to be recorded the name and address of the owner with the name of the land planner licensed land surveyor or registered professional engineer platting the tract 11 sites if any to be reserved or dedicated for parks playgrounds or other public uses 12 scale north arrow date and other pertinent data and so drawn that the north direction is to the top or left side of the map 13 contours with intervals of five feet or less shall be shown for the area all elevations on the contour map shall be referenced to the latest us coast and geodetic survey data 14 all physical features of the property to be subdivided including locations of all watercourses ravines bridges culverts existing structures and other features pertinent to subdivision the outline of wooded areas or the location of important individual trees may be required d plats to be marked as preliminary the following notice shall be placed on the face of each preliminary plat by the developer preliminary plat e city manager review of application the city manager shall make a study of the plat and give a report to the city planning commission before its final action on the preliminary plat f planning commission review the planning commission shall examine application plat and related material submitted for conformity to these regulations and may if necessary enter into negotiations with the subdivider on changes deemed advisable and the kind and extent of improvements to be made by him the commission shall thereafter submit its recommendation to the city council g action by city council the city council shall within 30 days after the filing of such preliminary plat act thereon as submitted or modified and if approved the city council shall express its approval as conditional approval and state the conditions of such approval if any or if disapproval shall express its disapproval and its reasons therefor the action of the city council shall be noted on two copies of the preliminary plat referenced and attached to any conditions required by the city council action of the city council shall be certified by the city clerk one copy shall be returned to the subdivider and the other retained in the files of the city h effect of conditional approval by city council conditional approval of a preliminary plat by the city council shall be deemed an expression of approval of the layouts submitted on the preliminary plat as a guide to the installation of streets water sewer and other required improvements and utilities and to the preparation of the final or record plat except as provided for herein approval of the preliminary plat shall constitute conditional approval of the final plat when all conditions of approval noted as provided in this section have been met no work shall be done on the subdivision before the final plat is accepted and recorded except with the written approval of the city council i term of conditional approval  expiration conditional approval of a preliminary plat shall be effective for one year unless reviewed by the city council in the light of new or significant information which would necessitate the revision of the preliminary plat if no development or change in requirements has occurred which would affect the proposed plat at the end of the year of an effective approval the city council may extend its approval another year without the submission of a new preliminary plat by reapproving the original preliminary plat no filing fee is required for such reapproval    arts iiib via 981971 final plat submission review and recording a size scale paper all final plats shall be printed on good grade processed paper blue line or direct black and white all final plats shall be submitted on sheets 24 inches by 36 inches and to a scale of not less than 90 feet to the inch or larger where more than one sheet is required to encompass the subdivision an index sheet 24 inches by 36 inches shall be filed showing the entire subdivision together with the complete dedication attests dates titles and seals on one sheet b required markings and permitted tables the exterior boundary of the subdivision shall be indicated by the distinct dash line and corner markers by individual symbols the length and bearing of all straight lines radii area lengths tangent lengths and central angles of all curves shall be indicated along the boundary line of the subdivision and each block all dimensions along the lines of each lot shall be shown the curve data pertaining to the block or lot boundary may be placed in a curve table at the base of the plat and prepared in the following manner curve table curve number description elements outer property line center line inner property line c title and owners adjoining properties lots and blocks streets and utility easements the final plat shall show 1 a title including the name of the addition or subdivision the names of the owner and engineer or surveyor the scale and location of the subdivision with reference to the original land grant or survey and the abstract number and north point with true or magnetic north 2 the names of all adjoining subdivisions the dimensions of all abutting lots lot and block numbers and accurate reference ties to courses and distances of at least two recognized land corners 3 the names and accurate locations of all streets adjoining abutting or within not more than 500 feet of the subdivision 4 the location and dimension of any utility easement adjoining or abutting the subdivision or proposed within the subdivision d survey monuments the description and location of all survey monuments placed in the addition or subdivision shall be shown e relationship to preliminary plat the final plat shall conform to the preliminary plat as approved and shall incorporate all changes directions and additions imposed by the city council if so desired by the developer the final plat may constitute only that portion of the approved preliminary plat which he proposes to record and then develop  provided however that such portion conforms to all the requirements of these regulations f engineering plans engineering plans showing details of streets alleys culverts bridges storm sewers water mains sanitary sewers and other engineering details of the proposed subdivision shall be submitted to the city manager along with the final plat of the subdivision such plans shall be prepared by a registered professional engineer and shall conform to the design standards established by the city the final plat will not be released for filing until detailed engineering plans have been approved by the city council g certificates the following certificates must be submitted as indicated 1 ownership a certificate of ownership giving a metes and bounds description of the property dedication of all streets alleys parkways and parks where donated to the city and dedication or reservation of all easements and drainage ways to the public use signed and acknowledged before a notary public by the owner of the land shall appear on the face of the plat or index sheet of the plats where two or more sheets are required 2 survey the certificate of the licensed professional engineer or licensed public surveyor who surveyed mapped and monumented the land which certificates shall be attested before a notary public shall be placed on the face of the plan on index sheets of the plats together with the seals of the engineer or surveyor and notary public printed seals and signatures are prohibited except for extra prints that the owner or developer may need certified for other purposes the certificate of the engineer or surveyor to be placed on the plat shall be in the form approved by the city council from time to time a copy of which is on file in the office of the city clerk 3 taxes at the time the developer files the final plat with the city manager he shall also file a certificate showing that all taxes have been paid on the tract to be subdivided and that no delinquent taxes exist against the property h review by city manager and approval by city council upon receipt of the final plat accompanied by a final filing fee in the amount provided in the city fee schedule the city manager shall check the plat to ascertain its compliance with these regulations and the action of the city council when the copy of the final plat has been checked and found to meet all general requirements and design standards the developer or his engineers shall submit six copies of the final plat to the city manager the city manager shall stamp on each of the six copies the certificate of approval of the city council attested by the chairperson of the city council when such final plat has been approved i recording of final plats the developer or his authorized agent will secure the required number of plats and record them with the county clerks of dewitt or lavaca counties within 30 days of the date of the final approval  otherwise the approval of the city council becomes invalid two copies of the recorded final plat shall be returned immediately to the city manager    arts iiic vib 981971 secs 42364258  reserved article iii  design and construction standards streets a the arrangement character extent width grade and location of all streets shall conform to the city major thoroughfare plan and shall be considered in their relation to existing and planned streets to topographical conditions to public safety and in their appropriate relation to the proposed uses of the land to be served by such streets b when such streets are not on the major thoroughfare plan the arrangement of streets in a subdivision shall either provide for the continuation of appropriate projections of existing streets in surrounding areas or conform to a plan for the neighborhood approved or adopted by the city planning commission to meet a particular situation where topographical or other conditions make continuance or conformity to existing streets impracticable c minor streets shall be so laid out that their use by will be discouraged d if the subdivision abuts or contains an existing or proposed arterial street the city planning commission may require marginal access streets reverse frontage deep lots with rear service alleys or such treatment as may be necessary for adequate protection to residential properties and to afford separation of local traffic e reserve strips controlling access to streets shall be prohibited except where their control is definitely placed in the city under conditions approved by the city planning commission f street jobs with centerline offsets of less than 125 feet shall be avoided g arterial street intersections shall be at 90degree angles other street intersections shall be laid out so as to intersect as nearly as possible at right angles and no street shall intersect at less than 75 degrees h street rightofway widths shall be as shown on the master thoroughfare plan and if not shown therein shall be not less than as follows 1 primary or arterial thoroughfares maximum 90 feet depending upon the location and the city street plat with which the primary thoroughfare is to be connected 2 secondary thoroughfares 60 feet 3 minor residential streets 50 feet 4 access or service roads 40 feet 5 minor streets in apartment commercial or industrial areas 60 feet i half streets are prohibited except when essential to the reasonable development of the subdivision in conforming to the other requirements of these regulations and where the city council finds it will be practical to require the dedication of the other onehalf when the adjoining property is subdivided whenever a partial street exists along a common property line the other portion of the street shall be dedicated where part of a street is being dedicated along a common property line and the ultimate planned width is 50 feet the first dedication will be 30 feet  where the ultimate planned width is 60 feet the first dedication will be 35 feet j a culdesac shall not be longer than 600 feet and at the closed end shall have a turnaround having an outside roadway diameter of at least 80 feet and a street property line diameter of at least 90 feet k new streets of like alignment shall bear the names of existing streets and shall be dedicated at equal or greater widths than the existing streets no street name shall be used which will duplicate or be confused with the names of existing streets street names shall be subject to approval of the city council l all new streets dedicated within a subdivision shall be improved in accordance with specifications of the city    art iva 981971 alleys a alleys shall be provided in commercial and industrial districts except that the city council may waive this requirement where other definite and assured provision is made for service access such as offstreet loading unloading and parking consistent with and adequate for the use proposed service alleys in commercial and industrial districts shall be a minimum of 25 feet in width b in residential districts alleys if provided shall be parallel or approximately parallel to the frontage of the street alleys in residential districts shall be a minimum of 20 feet in width and must be covered by six inches of gravel c where the deflection of alley alignment exceeds 30 degrees a cutback of a minimum of 15 feet or of such greater distance as to provide safe vehicular movement shall be established on the inside property line and the alley if paved shall have the paving cut back in the same manner d deadend alleys shall be avoided where possible but if unavoidable shall be provided with adequate turnaround facilities at the deadend as determined by the city council    art ivb 981971 easements a easements shall be provided at the rear of lots not served by alleys running parallel or approximately parallel to the frontage of the street all easements in residential districts shall be a minimum of 20 feet in width b easements across lots or centered on side lot lines shall be provided for utilities where necessary and shall be of such widths as may be reasonably necessary for the utility using same c where a subdivision is traversed by a watercourse drainage way channel or street there shall be provided a storm easement or drainage rightofway conforming substantially with such course and of such additional width as may be designated by the city manager that will be reasonably adequate for the purpose parallel streets or parkways may be required in connection with this    art ivc 981971 blocks a the lengths widths and shapes of blocks shall be determined with due regard to provision of adequate building sites suitable to the special needs of the type of use contemplated zoning requirements as to lot sizes and dimensions and needs for convenient access circulation control and safety of street traffic b in general intersecting streets which determine the blocks lengths and widths shall be provided at such intervals as to serve cross traffic adequately and to meet existing streets or customary subdivision practices where no existing subdivision dictates the block length shall not exceed 1600 feet and shall generally be 1000 to 1200 feet in length where no existing subdivision dictates the block shall not be less than 500 feet in length  however in cases where physical barriers or property ownership creates conditions where it is appropriate that these standards be varied the length may be increased or decreased to meet the existing conditions having due regard for connecting streets circulation of traffic and public safety c where blocks in the vicinity of a school park or shopping center are platted 1000 feet or longer the city council may require a walkway near the middle of the block or at a street that terminates between the streets at the ends of the block the walkway shall not be less than four feet or more than eight feet in width shall have a fourfoot concrete walk block from sidewalk to sidewalk or to the rear property line if no street where no existing subdivision controls the block width or depth shall be platted to give lots with a depth to width ratio of generally not more than 212 to one and in no case more than four to one and the platting shall be such that the block width or depth generally shall not exceed 350 feet or be less than 215 feet when possible the block width and length shall be such as to allow two tiers of lots back to back to an alley d pedestrian walks not less than four feet wide shall be provided around the perimeter of all blocks    art ivd 981971 a conform to the minimum requirements of the established zoning district b each lot shall face on a public street c where corner lots are key lots that is where lots face the frontage street and also other lots face the side street the corner lot shall have a front building line on both streets d key lots or irregularly shaped lots shall have sufficient width at the building line to meet frontage requirements of the appropriate zoning district also the rear width shall be sufficient to provide access for all utilities including garbage collection but not less than ten feet e no lot shall be platted less than 90 feet in depth except in cases where an irregularly shaped tract is platted into lots and the remnant piece of property is of sufficient area to plat one or more lots the city council may waive the depth requirement to prevent a hardship on the developer f side lot lines shall be substantially at right angles or radial to street lines g double frontage and reverse frontage lots should be avoided except where essential to provide separation of residential development from traffic arteries or to overcome specific disadvantage of topography and orientation where lots have double frontage a front building line shall be established for each street h lot sizes may be increased from that originally platted provided that there is no remaining portion of a lot smaller than the original lot and that the final plat is submitted in accordance with the requirements of this article i in areas where the city sewer is not immediately available a lot shall be platted of such area as to meet the minimum requirements of the city pertaining to septic tank operation or applicable county health office standards the minimum area of any lot not served by the city sewer shall be 12000 square feet j no lot shall be replatted to reduce the size of the lots originally platted by a common dedicator unless the consent of all the property owners in the same addition has been obtained no lot will be reduced in width below a 50foot frontage with an area of 5000 square feet except for property having a local retail commercial or manufacturing zoning classification and not for residential use k when an applicant exhibits a duly executed and recorded deed covering a lot having dimensions of 50 feet by 90 feet or more which has been sold by metes and bounds prior to the passage of the ordinance from which this article is derived and such lot is being assessed for school taxes and conforms to the established lot pattern and zoning classification in the block where located then a building permit may be issued provided the requested use of such property conforms to the permanent zoning of the property covered by the application l subdivision plats for housing projects apartment areas shopping centers and industrial districts will not be required except in cases where dedications for streets street widening alleys or easements are required site plans shall be filed with the city for approval by the city council    art ive 981971 survey monuments in all subdivisions and additions corner monuments shall be established at the corner of each block in the subdivision consisting of an iron rod or pipe not less than threequarters inch in diameter and 24 inches deep set flush with the top of the sidewalk lot corner monuments shall be placed at all lot corners except corners which are also block corners consisting of iron rods or pipes of a diameter of not less than onehalf inch and 18 inches deep set flush with the top of the sidewalk in addition curve point markers shall be established of the same specifications as lot corner monuments    art vib 981971 building lines building lines shall be as shown on the final plat on all lots intended for business and residential use and shall provide the minimum setback as required by the zoning ordinance    art ivf 981971 public sites and open spaces a the subdivider may give consideration to suitable sites for schools parks playgrounds and other areas for public use so as to conform to the recommendations of the city council any provision for schools parks etc may be indicated on the preliminary plat b no individual partnership firm or corporation shall deepen widen fill reroute or change the course or location of any existing ditch channel stream or drainage way without first obtaining written permission of the city or other agency having jurisdiction c in cases where a subdivision contains or abuts a school park or playground the subdivider shall dedicate onehalf a normal residential street 25 feet and provide for onehalf the cost of paving and the full cost of all the utilities necessary the interested agency shall provide the necessary rightofway to make the street 60 feet in width which is 35 feet and provide onehalf the cost of the paving    art v 981971 improvements required prior to acceptance a monuments monuments shall be placed as required by this article b storm drainage an adequate storm sewer system consisting of inlets pipes and other underground drainage structures with approved outlets shall be constructed where runoff of storm water and the prevention of erosion cannot be accomplished satisfactorily by surface drainage facilities areas subject to flood conditions as established by the city will not be considered for development until adequate drainage has been provided c water all subdivisions shall be provided with an approved water system in the corporate limits of the city subdivisions shall be connected with the city water supply distribution system without cost to the city the subdivider shall install all water and sewer lines including customer services the engineer representing the subdivider shall prepare the plans and specifications for the water and sewer lines and present them to the city for approval before construction all construction shall be paid for by the subdivider meters will be installed by the water department in accordance with established tapping fees d street alley and sidewalk improvements 1 before approval and acceptance of any final plat the developer shall prepare or have prepared and submit three copies of the complete engineering plans of streets alleys curbs and gutters storm sewers and drainage structures and water and sanitary sewer improvements for the area covered by the final plat the developer shall have these plans prepared by his own engineers subject to approval of the plans by the city the city manager shall review the plans and specifications and if approved two sets shall be marked with the objections noted and returned to the developer for correction 2 after approval of the plat and of the plans and specifications the developer shall cause his contractor to install the facilities in accordance with the approved plans and specifications and these regulations the developer shall cause his engineer to design stake and supervise the construction of such improvements and shall cause his contractor to construct the improvements in accordance with these regulations the city shall consist only of domestic sewage properly shredded garbage industrial wastes and other wastes which are free from the prohibited constituents listed in section 4849 and limited in bod suspended delivered shall not exceed 200 ppm as determined by standard methods 3 hydrogen ion concentration ph of the sewage delivered shall be no lower than 60 nor higher than 90 and any acid wastes shall not
